# AI Index - Quick Reference

> **For AI Agents** - Essential context (30 lines)  
> **Full Details**: See individual policy documents

## Core Goals (4)
1. AI-Friendly: Parseable docs, clear routes, controlled context
2. Modular: Interchangeable, independent, stable I/O
3. Automated: Verifiable, scriptable, CI-ready
4. Orchestrable: Auto-discovery, routing, scheduling

## Safety Constraints (5)
| Constraint | Principle | Details |
|------------|-----------|---------|
| Path Access | Read routes, Write ownership | security_details.md Â§ 1 |
| Tool Calls | Whitelist, Default deny | security_details.md Â§ 2 |
| Database | Semi-auto, Human review | security_details.md Â§ 3 |
| Network | Default deny, Explicit | security_details.md Â§ 4 |

## Workflow (6 Steps)
S0: Refresh context â†’ S1: Task modeling â†’ S2: Plan review â†’ 
S3: Implementation â†’ S4: Doc update â†’ S5: PR review

## Routes (12 Topics)
See context_routes in agent.md for on-demand loading

**4. æ›´æ–°agent.mdæ–‡æ¡£è§„èŒƒ**
```markdown
## 3. Document Writing Rules

### Language Rules âœ¨æ–°å¢

**For AI Documentation**:
- Use **English** for all AI-consumed documents
- Files: agent.md (body), *-quickstart.md, AI_*.md, *.yaml (configs)
- Key fields must be English: role, action, tool, trigger, priority, severity

**For Human Documentation**:
- Use **Chinese (Simplified)** for human developers
- Files: README.md, *_GUIDE.md (complete versions), tutorials

**Mixed Content**:
- Keywords for triggers: Chinese + English (both for matching)
- Code comments: English preferred
- YAML comments: Chinese allowed for clarity

**Consistency**: One language per document (no mixing in body text)

**è¯¦è§**: `doc/process/AI_CODING_GUIDE.md` (English version)
```

**6. Scriptè§¦å‘æœºåˆ¶ç®¡ç†** â­ æ–°å¢

```yaml

version: "1.0"
description: "Centralized script execution triggers configuration"

# PRè§¦å‘ï¼ˆé˜»å¡å¼ï¼‰
on_pull_request:
  blocking:
    - script: agent_lint.py
      description: "Validate agent.md YAML"
      timeout: 60
    - script: doc_route_check.py
      description: "Verify routes"
      timeout: 30
    - script: db_lint.py
    - script: contract_compat_check.py
    ...
  
  non_blocking:
    - script: doc_style_check.py
      allow_failure: true

# å®šæœŸè§¦å‘
on_schedule:
  daily:
    - script: health_check.py
      cron: "0 2 * * *"
      alert_threshold: 80
    - script: ai_maintenance.py
      cron: "0 3 * * *"
  
  weekly:
    - script: dataflow_trace.py
      cron: "0 4 * * 0"

# æ‰‹åŠ¨è§¦å‘
manual:
  - script: workflow_suggest.py
    parameters:
      - name: PROMPT
        required: true
  - script: dataflow_visualize.py
    parameters:
      - name: FORMAT
        default: "mermaid"

# Git Hooks
on_commit:
  pre_commit:
    - script: doc_route_check.py
  pre_push:
    - script: agent_lint.py

# æ¡ä»¶è§¦å‘
conditional:
  - script: frontend_types_check.py
    trigger_on:
      files_changed: ["tools/openapi.json"]
  - script: migrate_check.py
    trigger_on:
      files_changed: ["db/engines/**/*.sql"]
```

**1. å¥åº·åº¦æ£€æŸ¥ä¸»è„šæœ¬**

**åˆ›å»º**: `scripts/health_check.py`ï¼ˆçº¦600è¡Œï¼Œè‹±æ–‡æ³¨é‡Šï¼‰

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Project Health Check System
Evaluate project health across 5 dimensions with weighted scoring
"""

class HealthChecker:
    def __init__(self, model_path='doc/process/HEALTH_CHECK_MODEL.yaml'):
        self.model = self.load_model(model_path)
        self.results = {}
        self.issues = []
    
    def run_all_checks(self):
        """Run all dimension checks"""
        for dimension in self.model['health_dimensions']:
            dim_name = dimension['dimension']
            self.results[dim_name] = self.check_dimension(dimension)
    
    def check_dimension(self, dimension):
        """Check single dimension"""
        scores = []
        for metric in dimension['metrics']:
            score, issue = self.run_metric_check(metric)
            scores.append(score * metric['weight'])
            if issue:
                self.issues.append(issue)
        return sum(scores)
    
    def run_metric_check(self, metric):
        """
        Run single metric check
        Returns: (score: float 0-100, issue: dict or None)
        """
        # Execute check_command
        # Parse result
        # Compare with threshold
        # Return score and issue details
    
    def calculate_total_score(self):
        """Calculate weighted total score"""
        total = 0
        for dim in self.model['health_dimensions']:
            dim_name = dim['dimension']
            weight = float(dim['weight'].strip('%')) / 100
            total += self.results[dim_name] * weight
        return total
    
    def generate_report(self):
        """Generate reports in multiple formats"""
        # JSON: ai/health_reports/latest.json
        # Markdown: ai/health_reports/health-summary.md (AI doc)
        # HTML: doc/templates/health-dashboard.html (Human doc)
    
    def trend_analysis(self, days=30):
        """Analyze trends from historical data"""
        # Read ai/health_reports/history/*.json
        # Calculate 7-day, 30-day trends
        # Identify anomalies (drop > 5 points)
    
    def prioritize_issues(self):
        """Sort issues by severity and impact"""
        # Sort by: critical > high > medium > low
        # Generate top 5 recommendations
```
